<name>Randall Henderson</name>< date>
1569614463157< /date>

5</rate>
< review>
After too many years of whining and moaning about the light keeping us from a good night's sleep, we needed some way to seriously darken our master bedroom. And since our only experience was with hotels and cruise ships, we thought, "Hey, blackout drapes!" Perfect. The only solution. I went online, read the Reports for a number of businesses, and settled on Jacoby, because of its great rating. It was the first and last phone call I made. Cory arrived promptly a few days later to help me through the process of selecting and ordering blackout drapes for the master bedroom. I thought. Surprise! Blackout drapes were completely outside our budget. No, seriously, waaaaay outside our budget. I was stunned as Cory patiently explained the laborious process for manufacturing blackout drapes (e.g., they are always custom-made) and, consequently, their expense. I completely understood, but I was also beginning to reconcile myself to never having another good night's sleep. Then Cory brightened and said, "But there are alternatives that are less expensive." And then, for the next hour-and-a-half, she paraded ideas and samples before me, made suggestions, and "thought" out loud while she tried various solutions, rejecting some, setting aside others for consideration. It was fascinating watching and hearing her "process." At the end of our initial time together, I settled on a multicellular shade (something I had never heard of and didn't know existed). Cory gave me a date that the shades would be ready to be installed, and on that very day, I was called, an appointment was made, and a week later Gary came to install them. Happily, in the middle of it all, Cory dropped in, and we had a terrific visit while Gary finished up. There was a very minor glitch once the shade was in, but it had nothing to do with Cory's and Gary's work (and everything to do with the "abstract" geometry of my house - I don't think you could find a true right angle anywhere!). I must tell you that Gary immediately offered to return the shade to the factory and have them shave off a fraction of an inch, then return and reinstall it. I decided against that, to wait and see, and am very happy I did. The glitch turned out to be no glitch at all in terms of the shade's effectiveness. We are now happily cocooned in almost pitch-blackness at night (and sometimes during the day!), and both of us are sleeping much better. I cannot too highly recommend Cory and Gary Jacoby (and their "Company"). They are two extremely professional, very bright, and utterly delightful people. You could not put yourself/yourselves into better hands.< /review>

<Review>Just got home from this waste of time and wanted to hit this Yelp while still hot under the collar.  This review is for the LA Laser and Skin Center in Westwood.

I called and explained that my local dermatologist has prescribed the facial chemo cream from my pre-cancerous spots and sun damage.  However, this process is long and painful.  There is a great alternative called Photo Dynamic Therapy, or PDT, that is as effective, quicker, and less painful.  My dermatologist does not have the equipment but LA Laser advertises the procedure on their website so I made a consultation appointment.

Arrived at my appointment and was surprised that it was so quiet.  Not a patient in sight.  Great!  Who likes to wait?

Was ushered in by my “consultant” and I explained what I was there for.  She looked surprised and said that PDT was for cosmetic purposes and not skin cancer use.  I groaned inside when I heard her say this.  You can see for yourself that she is completely wrong by typing PDT and skin cancer into a google search.

She then said that she would need me to talk to a doctor (I expected nothing less) but that the doctor was trying to leave early and she would have to see if he had time.  I explained that I would appreciate that since I had driven over an hour to be there.

She came back in and said that the doctor would be too busy to see me (Really?  Because it was a ghost town in there!).  She also went on to explain again that the PDT therapy was only for cosmetic purposes (Wrong!) and I should schedule an appointment with a doctor (I thought I had already).  I declined, took my paperwork from them, and left.

Bottom line is, if they are this dis-organized, this lacking in knowledge, and this inconsiderate, you should probably get your work done somewhere else.

I feel I dodged a bullet and it only cost me a few gallons of gas.</Review>< rating>

< Review>
Not your usual Chinese food. If you ever wonder what’s food really like in China, I imagine is something like this place. Their juicy pork dumplings are spectacular and the Beef Wrap is quite the delicacy. They are also known for their hand tossed noodles and spicy chicken both of which are the right amount of spice and flavor.< /Review>

<name>Tony Fu<//name><time>1533522447430< /time><rate>5< /rate>< review>
We are happy to finally got a good Chinese noodle restaurant in the South Bay. Hand pull, knife cut wide noodles with good variety of flavors.

We had House special Beef Noodle soup (medium flat), and House style chow mien (knife cut) both were excellent.

If you like lamb, definitely try the Lamb skewers with exotic flavors. (3 in an order, we got 2 orders)

The XLB and Beef roll are both good but not extraordinary compared to the noodles. We ordered 3 appetizers, pig ears was the best.</review>

< Review>
I have lived in Spring Valley 30 years and feel KT Donuts are the best there are anywhere. A great community secret, especially if you are lucky enough to get a fresh hot batch of their glazed donuts around 8:30pm each night. Literally melts in your mouth...be careful not to eat a whole dozen! This family takes extreme pride in creating amazingly fresh and delicious donuts as well as servicing everyone in a positive cheerful manner. There are more expensive shops and wider varieties but none have that "homemade, old school favor" of KT's donuts. Take it from an experienced donut aficionado...this place is donut heaven!</Review>

Suzy must really love her work. All staff are over the top cheerful and informed. Food is as expected from this chain. However, I requested a custom burger based on the Butter Jack. Here's where Suzy came in. As I took a seat she appeared tableside to get clarification on my order. She then  walked it back to the kitchen (which is on full display). As I waited, the details of the brand new ground up remodel. The techno-cube architecture works well with the frosted aluminum windows and doors, and serve to blend in with grey and river stone paint, hiteck lighting and you get a clean and bright atmosphere.
